<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">PRODUCTION
COSTS RELATED TO SALES. Production costs related to sales for the three and six 
months ended June 30, 2015 were $20,000 and $45,000,
respectively. These are expenses are directly related to the milling, packaging 
and shipping of gold and other precious metals
product. Costs were nominal in 2<SUP>nd</SUP> quarter, 2015 as the Company was 
engaged in the final stages of mine and mill preparation
in order to commence consistent operations. Production costs related to sales 
for the three and six months ended June 30, 2014
were $105,993 and $105,993, respectively. As the Company was not conducting 
consistent operations in the 1<SUP>st</SUP> Quarter
of 2014, therefore, only costs incurred in 2<SUP>nd</SUP> quarter.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">MINE
OPERATING COSTS. Mine operating costs for the three and six months ended June 
30, 2015 were $40,000 and $95,000, respectively.
These costs are directly related to the extraction of mine tonnage to be 
processed at the mill. Mine operating costs for the three
and six months ended June 30, 2014 were $56,453 and $56,453, respectively. 
Again, the main reason for low mining costs in the
1<SUP>st</SUP> and 2<SUP>nd</SUP> quarters of 2014 is that San Pablo mine was 
being rehabilitated during the period, and little
test mining activity was conducted.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">PRE-PILOT
PRODUCTION EXPENSES. Pre Pilot-Production Expenses for the three and six months 
ended June 30, 2015 were $316,406 and $800,561,
respectively. The decrease in expense in 2015 was due to the Company focusing on
the final stages of mine and mill preparation
and improvements in order to commence and maintain consistent operations; and 
negotiating the financing in order to fund consistent
operations (See financing agreement with Golden Post Rail LLC., above). Pre 
Pilot-Production expenses for the three and six months
ended June 30, 2014 were $23,833 and $844,179, respectively. During the 
1<SUP>st</SUP> quarter 2014, the San Pablo mine and the
pilot mill facility were prepared for initial test operations, and significant 
pre-pilot production expenses were incurred. These
pre-pilot production costs were nominal in the 2<SUP>nd</SUP> quarter 2014, as 
initial test operations were in process.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">PROPERTY
HOLDING COSTS. Property holding costs for the three and six months ended June 
30, 2015were $116,705 and 236,317, respectively.
These costs are concessions taxes, leases on land and other direct costs of 
maintaining the San Jose de Gracia property. These
costs were accounted for as Exploration Costs in the 1<SUP>st</SUP> quarter of 
2014 and re-classed to property holding costs in
the 2<SUP>nd</SUP> quarter 2014 and amounted to 287,023.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">GENERAL
AND ADMINISTRATIVE EXPENSES. Operating expenses for the three and six months 
ended June 30, 2015 were $377,966 and $720,642, respectively.
In 2015, this included $435,000 in expenses related to issuance of share based 
compensation. The above expenses include depreciation
and amortization amounts of $6,100 and $17,810 for the three and six months 
ended June 30, 2015, respectively.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">OTHER
INCOME (EXPENSE). Other income, exclusive of currency transaction gain or (loss)
for the three and six months ended June 30, 2015
was $(431,295) and $(1,004,704), respectively. Currency transaction gain or 
(loss) was $(381,854) and $(844,683) for the three
and six months ended June 30, 2015, respectively. The reason for this increased 
loss is the devaluation of the Mexican Peso in
2015. Other income, exclusive of currency transaction gain or (loss) for the 
three and six months ended June 30, 2014 was $(143,140)
and $(91,329), respectively. Currency gain/(loss) was $(87,068) and $6,974 for 
the three and six months ended, respectively.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">NON-CONTROLLING
INTEREST. The non-controlling interest portion of the net loss for the three and
six months ended June 30, 2015 was $(53,879)
and $(117,069), respectively.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">COMPREHENSIVE
INCOME (LOSS). Comprehensive income (loss) includes the Company&#8217;s net
income (loss) plus the unrealized currency translation
gain (loss) for the period. For the three and six months ended June 30, 2015, 
the Company recorded a gain (loss) of $(336,591)
and $(1,071,345), respectively.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt"><FONT 
STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>Liquidity
and Capital Resources</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">As
of June 30, 2015, the Company had working capital of $4,312,597, comprised of 
current assets of $6,395,670 and current liabilities
of $2,083,073. This represents an increase of $5,238,128 from the working 
capital (deficit) maintained by the Company of $(925,531)
as of December 31, 2014, due primarily to the closing of the financing agreement
with Golden Post Rail, LLC, and due to sales
of common stock during the period. Net cash (used) in operations for the six 
months ended June 30, 2015 was $(2,361,383) compared
with $(2,098,604) for the six months ended June 30, 2014. In the 2014 period, 
net cash used was primarily related to the preparation
of the San Pablo mine and pilot mill facility in order to commence test mining 
and milling operations; while in the 2015 period,
the next cash used was related to currency loss ($800,000), pre pilot production
expenses (payroll and activities in the mine
and mill), and general and administrative expenses.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">As
the Company was able to close financing agreements in the second quarter 2015, 
it will now be engaged in improving and expanding
its test mining and milling operations at San Jose de Gracia.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Net
cash provided by (used) in investing activities for the six months ended June 
30, 2015 and 2014 was $81,466 and $(78,680), respectively.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Net
cash provided by financing activities for the six months ended June 30, 2015 and
2014 was $3,539,250 and $1,455,000, respectively.
The primary components for the current year are for common share purchases of 
$2,917,750. Proceeds will be used to improve mining
and milling operations, and to prepare to process bulk mined samples through the
mill facility. In the prior year, the primary
component was issuance of preferred shares, Series B for cash of 
$1,101,000.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif"><B>Noncontrolling
Interest</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Under
the terms of the Earn In Agreement (September 1, 2006 to March 15, 2011), 
Goldgroup Mining Inc. and its wholly owned subsidiary
Goldgroup Resources, Inc. (Goldgroup), through 2010, had contributed capital to 
DynaM&eacute;xico in order to acquire 25% of the
outstanding shares (a shareholder interest) of DynaResource de M&eacute;xico, 
S.A. de C.V. (DynaM&eacute;xico). In March 2011,
Goldgroup had contributed a total of $18 M USD capital to DynaM&eacute;xico in 
order to acquire a total of 50% of the outstanding
shares (a shareholder interest) of DynaM&eacute;xico. From March 2011 through 
May 2013, Goldgroup owned 50% of the outstanding
shares of DynaM&eacute;xico, and since May 2013 to current date Goldgroup owns 
20% of the outstanding shares of DynaM&eacute;xico.
The applicable portion of the earnings or loss attributable to Goldgroup is 
offset in this section. For the three and six months
ended June 30, 2015, the portion of the net loss attributable to Goldgroup was 
$(53,879) and $(117,069), respectively.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt 10pt; text-
align: justify; text-indent: -10pt"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, 
Times, Serif"><B>Off-Balance
Sheet Arrangements&#9;</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">As
of June 30, 2015, we did not have any off-balance sheet arrangements (as that 
phrase is defined by SEC rules applicable to this
report) which have or are reasonably likely to have a material adverse effect on
our financial condition, results of operations
or liquidity.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt"><FONT 
STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>Plan
of Operation</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
Plan of operation for the next twelve months includes DynaMineras continuing the
improvement and expansion of the pilot production
mining and milling operations at SJG, utilizing the proceeds from the recent 
sale of equity and the proceeds from the financing
agreement with Golden Post Rail LLC. The Company funds its general and 
administrative expenses in the US. The Company&#8217;s
operating subsidiaries, DynaMineras and DynaOperaciones, receive monthly fees 
for management of SJG activities and personnel.
These amounts are eliminated in consolidation. The Company believes that cash on
hand, and including financing arrangements agreed
to, is adequate to fund its ongoing general and administrative expenses through 
2015. The Company plans to seek additional debt
funding during the next 12 months depending on results of pilot production 
activities, market conditions, and other factors.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt"><FONT 
STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>Capital
Expenditures</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
Company&#8217;s primary activities relate to the exploitation of the SJG 
property through its 100% owned operating subsidiary,
DynaMineras. DynaMineras is conducting activities at SJG under the terms of the 
Exploitation Amendment Agreement (the &#8220;EAA&#8221;,
or, &#8220;operating agreement&#8221;) with DynaM&eacute;xico. The Company plans
to acquire necessary or optional equipment in
the immediate future, in order to facilitate the test mining and pilot milling 
operations and is budgeting $2,000,000 for these
purposes.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>No
Known Reserves</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
SJG property is without known reserves. Under U.S. standards, mineralization may
not be classified as a &#8220;reserve&#8221;
unless a determination has been made that the mineralization could be 
economically and legally produced or extracted at the time
the reserve determination is made.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif"><B>Capital
Advances to Subsidiaries</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif"><B><I>DynaResource
de M&eacute;xico S.A. de C.V. 
(&#8220;DynaM&eacute;xico&#8221;)</I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B><I>Equity
Ownership of DynaM&eacute;xico</I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">In
May 2013, the Company acquired additional shares in the outstanding equity in 
DynaM&eacute;xico in exchange for the retirement
of accounts receivable of $2,393,803, which amount was due from 
DynaM&eacute;xico at December 31, 2012. As a result, the Company
currently owns 80% of the outstanding equity of DynaM&eacute;xico.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B><I>Amounts

from DynaM&eacute;xico. As a result, and at June 30, 2015;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:

from Goldgroup Mining Inc. (&#8220;Goldgroup&#8221;) to 
Dyna<I>M&eacute;xico</I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">In
2014, Goldgroup advanced $111,500 to DynaM&eacute;xico and in 2013 Goldgroup 
advanced $120,000 USD to DynaM&eacute;xico. This
total $231,500 is being carried by DynaM&eacute;xico at June 30, 2015 as a Due 
to Non-Controlling Interest.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>Note
Receivable &#8211; Affiliate</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 12pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif">DynaResource
Nevada, Inc., a Nevada Corporation (&#8220;DynaNevada&#8221;), with one 
operating subsidiary in M&eacute;xico, DynaNevada de M&eacute;xico,
S.A. de C.V. (&#8220;DynaNevada de M&eacute;xico&#8221;) have common officers, 
directors and shareholders. The total amount loaned
by the Company to DynaNevada at December 31, 2010 was $805,760. The terms of the
Note Receivable provided for a &#8220;Convertible
Loan,&#8221; repayable at 5% interest over a 3 year period, and convertible at 
the Company&#8217;s option into Common Stock of
DynaNevada at $0.25 / Share.&nbsp;&nbsp;On December 31, 2010, the Company 
converted its receivable from DynaNevada into 3,223,040
Shares of DynaNevada; and as a result, the Company owns 19.92% of the 
outstanding share capital of DynaNevada. DynaNevada is a
related entity, and through its subsidiary in M&eacute;xico (DynaNevada de 
M&eacute;xico), (&#8220;DynaNevada de M&eacute;xico&#8221;),
has entered into an Option agreement with Grupo M&eacute;xico 
(&#8220;IMMSA&#8221;) in M&eacute;xico, for the exploration and
development of approximately 3,000 hectares in the State of San Luis Potosi 
(&#8220;the Santa Gertrudis Property&#8221;). In March,
2010, DynaNevada de M&eacute;xico completed the Option with IMMSA so that it now
owns 100% of Santa Gertrudis. In June, 2010,
DynaNevada de M&eacute;xico acquired an additional 6,000 Hectares in the State 
of Sinaloa (&#8220;the San Juan Property&#8221;).
The Company has loaned additional funds to DynaNevada since 2010 for maintenance
of concessions and other nominal required fees
and expenses. The Company currently has a receivable from DynaResource Nevada, 
Inc. of $167,666 and an investment balance of $70,000
as of June 30, 2015.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt"><FONT 
STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-transform: 
uppercase"><B>Item
4.&#9;Controls and Procedures</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt"><FONT 
STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><U>Evaluation
of Disclosure Controls and Procedures</U></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
company carried out an evaluation of the effectiveness of the design and 
operation of its disclosure controls and procedures (as
defined in Exchange Act Rules&nbsp;13a-15(e) and 15d-15(e)) as of June 30, 2015.
This evaluation was accomplished under the supervision
and with the participation of our chief executive officer / principal executive 
officer, and chief financial officer / principal
financial officer who concluded that the company&#8217;s disclosure controls and
procedures are effective to ensure that all material
information required to be filed in the quarterly report on Form 10-Q has been 
made known to them.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">For
purposes of this section, the term disclosure controls and procedures means 
controls and other procedures of an issuer that are
designed to ensure that information required to be disclosed by the issuer in 
the reports that it files or submits under the Act
(15 U.S.C. 78a et seg.) is recorded, processed, summarized and reported, within 
the time periods specified in the Commission&#8217;s
rules and forms. Disclosure, controls and procedures include, without 
limitation, controls and procedures designed to ensure that
information required to be disclosed by in our reports filed under the 
Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &quot;Act&quot;)
is accumulated and communicated to the issuer's management, including its 
principal executive and principal financial officers,
or persons performing similar functions, as appropriate to allow timely 
decisions regarding required disclosure.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Based
upon an evaluation conducted for the period ended June 30, 2015, our Chief 
Executive Officer and Chief Financial Officer as of
June 30, 2015, and as of the date of this Report, have concluded that as of the 
end of the period covered by this report, we have
identified no material weakness in our internal controls.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Corporate
expenditures are processed and paid by officers of the Company. However, the 
current number of transactions incurred by the Company
does not justify additional accounting staff to be retained.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt"><FONT 
STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><U>Changes
in Internal Controls over Financial Reporting</U></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
Company has not made any changes in its internal controls over financial 
reporting that occurred during the period covered by&nbsp;this
report on Form 10-Q that have materially affected, or is reasonably likely 
to&nbsp;materially affect, its internal control over
financial reporting.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 12pt; text-
align: center"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>PART
II</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt"><FONT 
STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>ITEM
1. &#9;<FONT STYLE="text-transform: uppercase">Legal 
Proceedings</FONT></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>US
Litigation (Dallas, Texas) &#8211; Company as Plaintiff</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">On
December 27, 2012, the Company, and DynaM&eacute;xico, filed an Original 
Petition and Application for Temporary Injunction and
Permanent Injunction in the 14<SUP>th</SUP> Judicial District Court of Dallas, 
Texas (the &#8220;Petition&#8221;) against Defendants
Goldgroup Mining Inc., Goldgroup Resources Inc., and certain individuals acting 
in concert with Goldgroup (collectively &#8220;Goldgroup&#8221;).
The Petition alleged, among other things, that Goldgroup has wrongfully used 
property, confidential information and data belonging
to DynaM&eacute;xico and consistently failed to disclose several matters of 
material importance to the public.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
Petition requested that Goldgroup be enjoined from: (a) using or disseminating 
any confidential information belonging to DynaM&eacute;xico,
(b) asserting that Goldgroup owns any interest in the San Jose de Gracia 
Project, rather than owning a common shares equity interest
in DynaM&eacute;xico, (c) improperly disclosing that Goldgroup is the operator 
of the San Jose de Gracia Project, rather than
Mineras de DynaResource S.A. de C.V. (&#8220;MinerasDyna&#8221;), and (d) 
failing to properly disclose that broad powers of attorney
for acting on behalf of DynaM&eacute;xico are held by a DynaUSA senior 
executive.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
Petition further requested, among other things: (a) a temporary and permanent 
injunction; (b) declaratory relief; (c) disgorgement
of funds alleged to have been improperly raised as a consequence of 
Goldgroup&#8217;s wrongful actions; (d) cancellation of shares
of DynaM&eacute;xico stock held by Goldgroup; and, (d) actual and punitive 
damages.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">At
the time of the filing, the Company believed the Petition to be necessary in 
order to protect its shareholder interests in DynaM&eacute;xico
and in order to protect the property, data, and assets of 
DynaM&eacute;xico.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Although
Goldgroup challenged the jurisdiction to the filed litigation in Texas, 
Goldgroup has acknowledged that it owns no direct interest
in the San Jose de Gracia Property, and it has acknowledged that Mineras de 
DynaResource SA de C.V. (&#8220;MinerasDyna&#8221;),
DynaUSA&#8217;s 100% owned subsidiary, is the exclusive operator of the San Jose
de Gracia Project.&nbsp; Additionally, recent
developments in M&eacute;xico in 2013, including: (1) the signing of the 
Exploitation Amendment Agreement (&#8220;EAA&#8221;)
between MinerasDyna and DynaM&eacute;xico; (2) the signing of a 20 year land 
lease agreement between MinerasDyna and the Santa
Maria Ejido Community surrounding the San Jose de Gracia Project; and (3) the 
acquisition by DynaUSA of a majority interest in
DynaM&eacute;xico; protect against Goldgroup&#8217;s wrongfully obtaining and/or
disseminating confidential data and information
of DynaM&eacute;xico.&nbsp; These recent developments in M&eacute;xico provided 
that the DynaResource Parties non-suited the Texas
action as announced by the Company on March 14, 2014, without prejudice to 
asserting or consolidating claims in M&eacute;xico,
as well as to contemplate additional claims or regulatory actions against 
Goldgroup in Canada.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>Litigation(s)
in M&eacute;xico &#8211; Company is Plaintiff</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
Company, and DynaM&eacute;xico have filed several legal actions in M&eacute;xico
against Goldgroup Mining Inc, Goldgroup Resources
Inc., certain individuals employed or previously employed by Minop, S.A. de C.V.
(a Company operating in M&eacute;xico and associated
with Goldgroup Mining Inc.), and certain individuals retained as agents of 
Goldgroup Mining Inc. The Company and DynaM&eacute;xico
are plaintiffs in the actions filed in M&eacute;xico and the outcomes are 
pending.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>Arbitration
filed by Goldgroup</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">On
March 14, 2014, Goldgroup filed for arbitration, citing the Earn In Agreement 
dated September 1, 2006. The Company filed an answer
on April 10, 2014 disputing that any issues exist which provide for 
arbitration.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">On
December 9, 2014, DynaM&eacute;xico filed a legal complaint against Goldgroup 
and the American Arbitration Association (&#8220;AAA&#8221;),
which seeks to terminate the arbitration proceedings. (See 
&#8220;DynaM&eacute;xico filed complaint against Goldgroup&#8221; 
below).</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">At
August 13, 2015, the Company continues to vigorously defend its position in the 
Arbitration proceedings, which is that no issues
exist between the parties which are available for arbitration.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>Complaint
filed by Goldgroup against the May 17, 2013 Shareholders Meeting of 
DynaM&eacute;xico</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">On
February 2, 2014, Goldgroup Resources Inc. filed a petition with the judge, 
tenth district Mazatlan, according to record 08/2014,
in the ordinary commercial action, against DynaResource Inc. and DynaResource de
M&eacute;xico, S.A. de CV. Goldgroup complains
against the results of the shareholders meeting of May 17, 2013, and petitions 
for the nullification of the meeting itself and
for the nullification of the additional shares of the outstanding capital of 
DynaM&eacute;xico issued to DynaResource, Inc. in
satisfaction of debts owed.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">DynaResource,
Inc. and DynaM&eacute;xico expect to vigorously defend all such complaints by 
Goldgroup, as there exists no legal basis for the
complaint against the May 17, 2013 shareholders meeting of 
DynaM&eacute;xico.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"></FONT></P>
<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 23 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt 
solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; 
width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: 
left"><TD STYLE="width: 100%; text-align: right"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type:

    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom:

    <!-- Field: /Page -->
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif"><B>DynaM&eacute;xico
filed Complaint against Goldgroup</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">On
December 9, 2014 DynaM&eacute;xico filed an Ordinary commercial lawsuit (Civil 
Claims), against Goldgroup Mining Inc., Goldgroup
Resources Inc. (&quot;Goldgroup&quot;, a shareholder of DynaM&eacute;xico); and,
against the American Arbitration Association
(&quot;AAA&quot;); based at the Thirty Sixth Civil Court in the Federal District
of M&eacute;xico, under file 1120 number / 2014
(&quot;the DynaM&eacute;xico Trial&quot;). The DynaM&eacute;xico Trial seeks to 
terminate the arbitration proceedings as DynaM&eacute;xico
believes there is no legal basis for arbitration, and the DynaM&eacute;xico 
Trial requests substantial damages are awarded DynaM&eacute;xico
from and against Goldgroup for:</FONT></P>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-
align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt 
Times New Roman, Times, Serif">a)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">wrongfully
                                         using and disseminating confidential 
information and data belonging to DynaM&eacute;xico;</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-
align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt 
Times New Roman, Times, Serif">b)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">asserting
                                         that Goldgroup owns any interest in the
San Jose de Gracia Project in northern Sinaloa,
                                         M&eacute;xico (&#8220;SJG 
Project&#8221;), rather than accurately disclosing that Goldgroup
                                         owns a common shares equity interest 
(shareholder&#8217;s interest) in DynaM&eacute;xico;
                                         </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-
align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt 
Times New Roman, Times, Serif">c)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">improperly
                                         disclosing the percentage of common 
shares equity interest (shareholder&#8217;s interest)
                                         owned by Goldgroup in 
DynaM&eacute;xico;</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-
align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt 
Times New Roman, Times, Serif">d)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">improperly
disclosing or implying that Goldgroup 
is the operator of the San Jose de Gracia Project;</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-
align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt 
Times New Roman, Times, Serif">e)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">attempting
                                         to delay, stop, or otherwise impair the
financing of, and further development of, the
                                         SJG Project; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-
align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt 
Times New Roman, Times, Serif">f)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">making
                                         numerous threats against 
DynaM&eacute;xico management and officers; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-
align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt 
Times New Roman, Times, Serif">g)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">failing
                                         to properly disclose that broad powers 
of attorney for acting on behalf of DynaM&eacute;xico
                                         are held by an individual not 
affiliated with Goldgroup.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif">DynaM&eacute;xico
believes the filing of the DynaM&eacute;xico Trial to be necessary in order to 
protect the property and interests of DynaM&eacute;xico,
and in order to seek fair retribution and substantial damage amounts caused by 
Goldgroup against DynaM&eacute;xico and the SJG
Project.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
Company believes that no material adverse change will occur as a result of the 
legal actions taken, and the Company further believes
that there is little to no potential for the assessment of a material monetary 
judgment against the Company for legal actions
it has filed in M&eacute;xico. For purposes of confidentiality, the Company does
not provide more specific disclosure in this
Form 10-Q.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif"><B>DynaM&eacute;xico
Statements of Fact</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">In
recent years, Goldgroup has continuously and consistently misrepresented its 
interest, ownership, and position related to DynaM&eacute;xico
and the SJG Project. DynaM&eacute;xico does herein state and represent the 
following:</FONT></P>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-

<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt
Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: 
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">At
                                         no time has Goldgroup owned any 
interest in the SJG Project; rather its only ownership
                                         interests have been earned under 
agreement as a common shares equity interest (shareholder&#8217;s
                                         interest) of 
DynaM&eacute;xico;</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New

<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt

                                         currently owns 20% of the outstanding 
share capital of DynaM&eacute;xico;</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt"><FONT 
STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>ITEM
2. &#9;<FONT STYLE="text-transform: uppercase">Unregistered Sales of Equity 
Securities and Use of Proceeds</FONT></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
Company reports the following sales of equity securities during the quarterly 
period ending June 30, 2015:</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align:
justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
Company sold 1,020,000 common shares for cash at $2.50 per share. These stock 
issuances were accompanied by the issuance of 1,020,000
warrants, which are exercisable at $2.50 per share expiring December 31, 
2017.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 12pt; text-
align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">The
sales of the securities identified above were made pursuant to privately 
negotiated transactions that did not involve a public
offering of securities and, accordingly, the Company believes that these 
transactions were exempt from the registration requirements
of the Securities Act pursuant to Section 4(2) thereof. Each investor 
represented that such investor either (A) is an &#8220;accredited
investor,&#8221; (B) has such knowledge and experience in financial and business
matters that the investor is capable of evaluating
the merits and risks of acquiring the shares of the Company&#8217;s common stock
or preferred stock, or (C) has appointed an appropriate
person to act as the investor&#8217;s purchaser representative in connection 
with evaluating the merits and risks of acquiring
the securities. All of the foregoing securities are deemed restricted securities
for purposes of the Securities Act.</FONT></P>
